)@@G@@ THE 1108 DOCUMENT PROCESSOR (DOC) IS A SYSTEM PROCESSOR WHICH    @G@@@@TU
)@@G@@ PRODUCES A STANDARDIZED PRINTED LISTING OF A DOCUMENT.  A DOCUMENT     TV
)@@G@@@F@@@@ IS A SYMBOLIC ELEMENT IN THE STANDARD 1108 FORMAT, AND MAY BE    TW
)@@G@@@C@@@@ MANIPULATED WITH THE USUAL FUNCTIONS OF FURPUR.@[@@@@SPACE @F@@@@TX
)@@G@@ THE APPEARANCE OF THE FINISHED DOCUMENT MAY BE CONTROLLED IN FOUR@#@@@@TY

)@@G@@ONS (,SIDHL ETC.) @F@@@@  - DIVISIONAL CONTROL STATEMENTS (CHAPTERS, SECUA
)@@G@@TIONS, PARAGRAPHS)@E@@@@  - LISTING CONTROL STATEMENTS (SPACING, PAGE EJUB
)@@G@@ECTS ETC.)  @^@@@@  - EDITING (UPDATING.) @[@@@@SPACE @E@@@@ IN ADDITIONUC
)@@G@@ TO THE REGULAR FEATURES OF DOC, THIS DOCUMENT  @B@@@@ DESCRIBES THE FOLUD
)@@G@@LOWING NEW FEATURES:    @G@@@@       -  'G' OPTION TO REMOVE HYPHENATED UE
)@@G@@WORDS FROM INPUT ELEMENT.     @C@@@@       -  'R' OPTION TO ALIGN THE RIUF
)@@G@@GHT MARGIN. @D@@@@       -  'RIGHTM' (RIGHT MARGIN) CONTROL STATEMENT.  UG
)@@G@@@E@@@@       -  'UNHYPH' (REMOVE HYPHENATION) CONTROL STATEMENT.  @E@@@@UH
)@@G@@       -  THE MEANING OF THE 'H' OPTION HAS BEED CHANGED.   @F@@@@      UI
)@@G@@    THE PRESENCE OF THE 'H' OPTION ON THE PROCESSOR CALL    @F@@@@      UJ

)@@G@@XT COMPOSITION.   @F@@@@ THE DOC PROCESSOR FORMS LINES OF TEXT THAT APPEAD

)@@G@@INTED AND WRITTEN @^@@@@ TO THE OUTPUT ELEMENT. @^@@@@2RIGHT MARGIN ALIGAI
)@@G@@NMENT.@F@@@@ DOCUMENTS BEING PREPARED FOR PUBLICATION SHOULD BE PRINTED AJ
)@@G@@USING @F@@@@ THE RIGHT MARGIN ALIGNMENT OPTION.  THE ROUTINE PERFORMING AK
)@@G@@THIS  @F@@@@ FUNCTION ALIGNS ONLY THE PRINTED OUTPUT TO THE RIGHT MARGINAL
)@@G@@.  THE@F@@@@ IMAGE INSERTED INTO THE OUTPUT ELEMENT IS THE ORIGINAL IMAGAM
)@@G@@E     @F@@@@ BEFORE RIGHT ALIGNMENT.  THUS ANY SUBSEQUENT UPDATING OR TEAN
)@@G@@XT    @F@@@@ EDITING SHOULD BE DONE USING A LISTING WITHOUT RIGHT ALIGNMAO
)@@G@@ENT.  @#@@@@2HYPHENATION.     @E@@@@ AN AUTOMATIC HYPHENATION ROUTINE ISAP
)@@G@@ INCORPORATED IN THE DOC@E@@@@ PROCESSOR.  THE DESIGN OF THIS ROUTINE ISAQ
)@@G@@ BASED ON A PAPER,@G@@@@ 'METHOD FOR HYPHENATING AT THE END OF A PRINTEDAR
)@@G@@ LINE', BY RICH AND     @G@@@@ STONE; COMMUNICATIONS OF THE ACM, AUGUST,AS
)@@G@@ 1965, PAGE 444.  BECAUSE     @F@@@@ OF THE NATURE OF THIS HYPHENATION RAT
)@@G@@OUTINE, GRAMMATICALLY CORRECT @G@@@@ RESULTS ARE NOT GUARANTEED, AND SHOAU
)@@G@@ULD NOT BE EXPECTED.  DOCUMENTS     @F@@@@ BEING PREPARED FOR PUBLICATIOAV
)@@G@@N SHOULD NOT, THEREFORE, BE PRINTED @A@@@@ USING THE AUTOMATIC HYPHENATOAW
)@@G@@R.    @[@@@@SPACE @F@@@@ THE HYPHENATOR MAY BE ACTIVATED AND DEACTIVATEDAX
)@@G@@ BY THE H OPTION  @E@@@@ AND THE 'HYPHEN' CONTROL CARD AS DESCRIBED ABOVAY
)@@G@@E.  SHOULD  @E@@@@ ALTERATIONS TO THE TEXT REQUIRE REFORMATTING OF THE TAZ
)@@G@@EXT,  @F@@@@ HYPHENATED WORDS WILL BE JOINED TOGETHER AS NECESSARY.  THIBA
)@@G@@S     @F@@@@ FEATURE ALSO ALLOWS TEXT ON INPUT CARDS TO BE HYPHENATED ATBB
)@@G@@ THE  @E@@@@ END OF A CARD AS DESIRED.  THIS MEANS THAT A WORD WHICH IS BC
)@@G@@@F@@@@ NORMALLY HYPHENATED, SUCH AS 'RIGHT-HANDED', MUST NOT BE SPLIT ATBD
)@@G@@@F@@@@ THE END OF A CARD IN SUCH A WAY THAT THE DESIRED HYPHEN IS THE   BE
)@@G@@@ @@@@ LAST CHARACTER ON THE CARD.  @^@@@@2HYPHENATION REMOVAL.   @G@@@@BF
)@@G@@ ONCE A DOCUMENT HAS BEEN UPDATED USING THE HYPHENATION ROUTINE THE     BG
)@@G@@@F@@@@ HYPHENS REMAIN FIXED.  IF A SUBSEQUENT LISTING IS RUN WITHOUT THEBH
)@@G@@@F@@@@ 'H' OPTION, OR WITH THE 'HYPHEN OFF' CONTROL STATEMENT, THESE    BI
)@@G@@@F@@@@ HYPHENS WILL STILL APPEAR.  IN ORDER TO REMOVE THESE HYPHENS FROMBJ
)@@G@@@F@@@@ THE INPUT ELEMENT A NEW UPDATE MUST BE RUN USING THE 'G' OPTION. BK
)@@G@@@[@@@@EJECT @E@@@@ IF THERE IS A WORD ON THE RIGHT MARGIN WHICH IS NORMABL
)@@G@@LLY A @G@@@@ HYPHENATED WORD, SUCH AS 'RIGHT-HANDED', IT MAY BE RETAINEDBM
)@@G@@ IN THE     @G@@@@ FOLLOWING MANNER.  A 'HYPHEN ON' CARD MUST BE INSERTEBN
)@@G@@D IMMEDIATELY     @F@@@@ PRECEDING THE LINE, AND A 'HYPHEN OFF' CARD IMMBO
)@@G@@EDIATELY FOLLOWING@F@@@@ IT.  THESE TWO 'HYPHEN' CONTROL STATEMENTS SHOUBP

)@@G@@E PREVIOUS LINE WAS ALSO HYPHENATED IT WILL BE JOINED @F@@@@ CORRECTLY. BR

)@@G@@ENATION REMOVAL OPTION IS IN EFFECT IT SHOULD NOT BE  @F@@@@ USED ON TABBU

)@@G@@'UNHYPH ON' CONTROL STATEMENT RESTORES THE@C@@@@ ORIGINAL G OPTION RATHEBX
)@@G@@R THAN TURNING IT ON.   @A@@@@2INHIBITION OF TEXT COMPOSITION.    @E@@@@BY
)@@G@@ THE MOVEMENT OF TEXT TO FORM COMPLETE LINES IS HALTED UPON @E@@@@ RECOGBZ
)@@G@@NITION OF A CONTROL CARD, AND AT THE START OF A NEW   @F@@@@ PARAGRAPH. CA

)@@G@@F A NEW LINE IS BEGUN.  @[@@@@SPACE @F@@@@ THE START OF A NEW PARAGRAPH CC
)@@G@@IS RECOGNIZED BY THE OCCURRENCE OF A@E@@@@ CARD OF TEXT (I.E., NOT A CONCD
)@@G@@TROL CARD) ON WHICH THE FIRST @F@@@@ NON-BLANK CHARACTER IS NOT IN COLUMCE
)@@G@@N N.  THIS INCLUDES BOTH THE  @F@@@@ CASE OF INDENTATION TO THE RIGHT ANCF
)@@G@@D THAT OF EXTENSION TO THE    @F@@@@ LEFT.   FOR THIS REASON, ALL LINES CG

)@@G@@ 2    @E@@@@      TDLIB (TAPE/DISK LIBRARY) IS A DATA MANAGEMENT SYSTEM PY
)@@G@@@F@@@@ DESIGNED TO FACILITATE ACCOUNTING OF CATALOGUED TAPE AND DISK    PZ
)@@G@@@F@@@@ FILES.  THE INFORMATION KEPT FOR EACH TAPE AND DISK IS COMPOSED  QA
)@@G@@@F@@@@ OF THE PROGRAMMER'S NAME, ACCOUNT NUMBER AND CATALOGUE DATE.     QB
)@@G@@@F@@@@ FURTHER INFORMATION KEPT (AT THE TAPE LIBRARIAN'S DISCRETION) IS QC
)@@G@@@F@@@@ VARIABLE, AND CAN INCLUDE FLAGS (SUCH AS 'TAPE HAS BEEN REMOVED  QD
)@@G@@@F@@@@ FROM LIBRARY'), OR SPECIAL DESCRIPTIONS OF A TAPE (FOR INSTANCE, QE
)@@G@@@#@@@@ BOOT OR LIBS).   @]@@@@SPACE 2     @F@@@@      THE LIBRARY NEEDS QF
)@@G@@TWO FILES WHICH IT TRIES TO ASSIGN VIA    @F@@@@ CSF$   THEY ARE LIBRARYQG
)@@G@@*TAPEFILE AND LIBRARY*DISCFILE.  IF EITHER@E@@@@ OF THESE ASSIGNS FAIL, QH
)@@G@@AN ERROR MESSAGE IS PRODUCED AND THE@#@@@@ PROGRAM EXITS.   @[@@@@      QI
)@@G@@@E@@@@      THE LIBRARY IS SET UP FOR THE USER AS WELL AS FOR THE @E@@@@QJ
)@@G@@ LIBRARIAN, WITH MOST OF THE COMMANDS BEING PRIVILEDGED.    @]@@@@COLUMNQK
